It is possible to beat the elder dragon in hardcore mode with nothing but it will take a while, here are the steps:  1) Make sure you spawn in a box rather than the obsidian pillar outside of the end island (so you can break out of the box) [Alternatively, if you do spawn on a pillar outside the end island, anger an enderman, let it teleport to you and kill it so you can teleport to the end island  2)Next, make yourself to the obsidian pillars which hold the end crystals and break the obsidian to make a staircase to the top (this is the bit which takes the longest) - also make sure you donâ€™t get hit with dragons breath  3)After that, punch the end crystals  4)Then, repeat the last two steps for all the pillars (Alternatively you could also get ender pearls before making the staircase and pearl to the other obsidian pillars to break the end crystals)  5)Then wait for the dragon to perch and keep punching it until it dies

14:55 "why do these end city have beet seeds in the chests?" Beet seeds were added in update 0.8, however, you had to travel long distances into unloaded chunks at a time were horses didn't exist just to find the seeds, so when the ender update came out (version 1.0) they added beet seeds to the end city chests so that players could more easily find them

To anyone! The best place to mine is -58 and when you find diamonds mine on a direct straight line from the diamonds on coordinate. (Ex: positive x) if you don't find any diamonds in the next hundred blocks then you need to go FROM THE DIAMONDS on the (Ex: z coordinate) and you should find some. (it doesn't matter if it's Positive or Negative). I did this and in about 15 - 30 mins I got about 2 stacks. I would recommend a few stacks of torches, eff 3, 4, 5, unbreaking, 1, 2, 3 and a fortune 3 pick. Caves work but in the new update if diamonds spawn next to "Cave Air" they are most likely to be 1-3 veins, while in strip mining it tends to be 4-8 veins.

LTN, the iron helmet with protection four is the same as a diamond helmet with no protection. Each half of an armor bar is 4% less damage, each protection level is 1% more defense. Having a full set of unenchanted diamond armor drops the damage you take to 20%. Full protection 4 on each piece divides the damage you take by five once more. And on java, the durability armor has affects it's damage reduction.
